<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подчинение.html>подчине́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podčinénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подчинение.html>подчине́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подчинение.html>подчине́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подчинение.html>подчине́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>submission, subjecting</li>
<li>subjection</li>
<li>subordination

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:попасть.html>попа́сть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:подчинение.html>подчине́ние</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">popástʹ v <b>podčinénije</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">become subordinate</span></div></dd>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подчинить.html>подчини́ть</a> (10238)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">под-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чинить.html>чини́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">činítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подчинить.html>подчини́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podčinítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подчинять.html>подчиня́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to subordinate <i>(to)</i>, to place (under), to place under the command</li>
<li>to subdue
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подчинить.html>подчини́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свое́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:воля.html>воле</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podčinítʹ</b> svojéj vole</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to bend to one's will</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подчинить.html>подчини́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>себе́</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podčinítʹ</b> sebé</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to override</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to dedicate
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подчинить.html>подчини́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:жизнь.html>жизнь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>одно́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:цель.html>це́ли</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podčinítʹ</b> žiznʹ odnój céli</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">dedicate one's life to one cause</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">grammar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to subordinate</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подчинять.html>подчиня́ть</a> (19249)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подчинить.html>подчини́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podčinítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подчинять.html>подчиня́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podčinjátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подчинить.html>подчини́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to subordinate <i>(to)</i>, to place (under), to place under the command</li>
<li>to subdue
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подчинять.html>подчиня́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свое́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:воля.html>воле</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podčinjátʹ</b> svojéj vole</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to bend to one's will</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подчинять.html>подчиня́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>себе́</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podčinjátʹ</b> sebé</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to override</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to dedicate
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подчинять.html>подчиня́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:жизнь.html>жизнь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>одно́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:цель.html>це́ли</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podčinjátʹ</b> žiznʹ odnój céli</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">dedicate one's life to one cause</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">grammar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to subordinate</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подчиняться.html>подчиня́ться</a> (4319)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подчинять.html>подчиня́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podčinjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подчиняться.html>подчиня́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podčinjátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подчиниться.html>подчини́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to obey, to submit to, to surrender, to be subordinate to</li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подшить.html>подши́ть</a> (16344)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">под-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шить.html>шить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подшить.html>подши́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podšítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">подшива́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to hem</li>
<li>to sew on</li>
<li>to sew a sole on, to sole (a shoe)</li>
<li>to file (documents, etc.)</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">под-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штаны.html>штаны́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">štaný</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ники</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-niki</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подштанники.html>подшта́нники</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podštánniki</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> <abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подштанники.html>подшта́нников</a></b>, <i>plural only</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> plural only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> long underpants, long johns <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">worn either under normal clothing in cold weather, or as a night dress</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подъездной.html>подъездно́й</a> (28941)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подъезд.html>подъе́зд</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podʺjézd</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-но́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подъездной.html>подъездно́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podʺjezdnój</span>) (<i>no comparative</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> approach

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">под-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-езжа́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-jezžátʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to go (by vehicle)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

</p>
<ol><li>to drive up (to)

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:можно.html>мо́жно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ли.html>ли</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:подъезжать.html>подъезжа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сюда.html>сюда́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:автомобиль.html>автомоби́ле</a>?</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Móžno li <b>podʺjezžátʹ</b> sjudá na avtomobíle?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Can one drive a car here?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to drop in, to pay a short visit</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to get (round), to start a pick up line, to get on the right side (of)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ловко.html>ло́вко</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ней</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:подъезжать.html>подъезжа́ет</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Lóvko on k nej <b>podʺjezžájet</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He is getting round her very nicely; he is getting on the right side of her</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подъем.html>подъем</a> (3113)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Deverbal of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поднимать.html>поднима́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podnimátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The combining form <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">-ём</span> is the normal deverbal equivalent of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-нима́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nimátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>/<i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">има́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">imátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; compare archaic first singular present tense <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">емлю́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jemljú</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">има́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">imátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru">подъём</strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podʺjóm</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подъем.html>подъёма</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подъем.html>подъёмы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подъем.html>подъёмов</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подъемный.html>подъёмный</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>lifting, raise, raising</li>
<li>hoisting <i>(of a flag)</i></li>
<li>salvaging <i>(of a sunken ship)</i></li>
<li>ascent, rise, upgrade</li>
<li>climb <i>(of a plane)</i></li>
<li>slope, rise <i>(of a mountain)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:величина.html>величина́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:подъем.html>подъёма</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">veličiná <b>podʺjóma</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">up gradient</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>raising, development, upsurge</li>
<li>enthusiasm, animation</li>
<li>instep <i>(of a foot)</i></li>
<li>reveille</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">phonetics<span class="ib-comma">,</span> phonology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> height (of vowels)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гласный.html>гла́сный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:средний.html>сре́днего</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:подъем.html>подъёма</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">glásnyj srédnevo <b>podʺjóma</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">mid vowel</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">vowel of middle height</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неподъемный.html>неподъёмный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nepodʺjómnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подымать.html>подыма́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">podymátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поднять.html>подня́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">podnjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подъемник.html>подъёмник</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">podʺjómnik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подъемный.html>подъёмный</a> (14571)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подъемный.html>подъёмный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podʺjómnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Alternative spelling of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подъемный.html>подъёмный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podʺjómnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>подъ<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ём<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1*a.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-подъём-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:порядочный.html>-н</a></b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>подъ-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-ём-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:порядочный.html>-н</a></b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b> <sup> | Кузнецова, Ефремова, 1986 | </sup>.
</p>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подъехать.html>подъе́хать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podʺjéxatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подъезжать.html>подъезжа́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to drive up (to)

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to drop in, to pay a short visit</li>

<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ловко.html>ло́вко</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ней</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:подъехать.html>подъе́хал</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Lóvko on k nej <b>podʺjéxal</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He got round her very nicely; he got on the right side of her</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подыграть.html>подыгра́вший</a></b>
